## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="bef68-1912">Windows Server 2012 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bef68-1912">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bef68-1913">此類別包含 Windows Server 2012 的下列屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bef68-1913">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
